- [World's Most Effective Pet Paw Cleaner](https://indigopetco.com/products/worlds-most-effective-pet-paw-cleaner): Did you know that over 2 million people per year get sick from bacteria found on your dog's paws? The fact is each day your dog is walking through dirt, trash, urine, and feces. They then track these germs into your home, car, bed, and around your family. The germs on dog paws are responsible for infecting humans with staph, salmonella, e. coli, and a nasty stomach bacteria. Never fear your adventurous pup’s dirty paws again with the Indigopetco™️ World's Most Effective Pet Paw Cleaner. Now your best friend can have all the outdoor fun they want without tracking harmful bacteria into your home or vehicle. The Indigopetco™️ Pet Paw Cleaner Cup features soft, thick silicone bristles inside an easy-to-grip BPA-free tumbler that works like a small agitation washer for his paws. All you have to do is fill the cup with water, insert your dog's dirty paw, give the cup a few twists, and pull out a perfectly clean paw. Repeat three more times, dab them dry and you’re good to go! Both the cup and bristles are top-rack dishwasher safe for easy cleaning and sanitizing. Available in three colors (Blue, Green, Pink) SIZE GUIDE: MEDIUM- Fits paws up to 2.5 inches LARGE - Fits paws up to 3.5 inches Easy to use To use, add a little water, insert the muddy paw, do the twist, dab the paw dry, repeat for three more paws. To clean remove the lid and bristles (bristles unroll for easy cleaning) and rinse for next use. Gentle Silicone Bristles The gentle silicone bristles remove dirt & bacteria from your dog's paws. Keep them germs outside - not in your car or home! The Indigopetco™️ Pet Paw Cleaner is also 100% BPA free.
